# fix411 — New app icon (circular Free4Me neon logo)

**Version:** 1.35.9+410 → **1.35.10+411**
**Type:** Asset swap — replaces launcher/round/adaptive icons + TV banner. Binary patch (webp). No Dart logic change.
**Tag:** v1.35.10
**⚠️ APPLY ORDER:** stacks on **fix410** — apply fix410 first. The pubspec/changelog hunks expect origin/main at 1.35.9+410 (fix410's state). If fix410 is NOT being shipped, tell Claude to rebase this onto +409.

## What
- Replaces all Android icon densities (mdpi→xxxhdpi) for `ic_launcher`, `ic_launcher_round`, and the adaptive `ic_launcher_foreground` with the circular neon "Free4Me" logo (source: the round transparent art).
- Adaptive background color `#FFFFFF → #000000` (matches the disc; masked corners read as black).
- Checkerboard backdrop removed; disc masked to a clean circle, content centered so phone circle/squircle masks do not clip the logo or text.
- `android:banner` (Android TV / Leanback) already points at `@mipmap/ic_launcher`, so the TV banner updates with it. (Banner remains square, unchanged behaviour.)

## A. Patch — APPLY (binary)

## Release — EXECUTE
CI owns `version.json` — do NOT run `update_version_json.py` or commit `version.json` before tagging. The release block only pushes `main` and runs `build_and_release.sh`.

```bash
git commit -m "fix411: new app icon (v1.35.10+411)"
git push origin main
./scripts/build_and_release.sh
```
